lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span text1;">自本月度报告的第<span lang="EN-US">101</span>期起，本报告全新改版。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">中国人权捍卫者（<span lang="EN-US">CHRD</span>）</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">所属的</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: mso-themecolor: text1;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">已将本网月度报告中所涉及的良心犯均全部收录，因此，我们从<span lang="EN-US">101</span>期起，将绝大多数本月没有动态信息的良心犯简历不再在月度报告里显示。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">查询所有相关信息，非常便捷。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">《中国大陆良心犯数据库》不但收录了目前在押的这个良心犯、政治犯，已经获释、死亡的良心犯、政治犯也在此数据库中可以查询到。《中国大陆良心犯数据库》收集工作整理自<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月开始，截至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">02</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日共 收录良心犯资料共<span lang="EN-US">3672</span>人。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">本报告主要关注的对象是所有在押的政治犯、良心犯——这里包括已被判刑的和羁押未判的——所有我们能够收集到确切信息的政治犯、良心犯。本报告竭力就包括汉、藏、维、哈萨克、回、蒙古、朝鲜、满等中国大陆多族裔政治犯、良心犯在内的信息进行收集、撰写和编辑，力求全面真实反映当前中国大陆政治犯、良心犯的恶劣的生存境遇。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">本报告为了便于人们查询检索，完全以良心犯、政治犯的姓名拼音顺序制作了完整的在押人员名录。同时，本报告仍对所有良心犯、政治犯的刑期进行了统计，羁押未判的也全部列于最后。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">本报告名单人员一旦取保候审、保外就医、无罪释放、回家监视居住、缓刑或刑满释放，都将从报告正式在押名单中移除，但其简历将显示于本期报告中。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">本报告每月不辍，期期更新，其中凝聚了许多义工、信息员和编辑长期以来默默无闻的辛劳和奉献。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">9</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">年多来，本网一共收集、整理、编辑过的有较为翔实资料的人员名单及其简历超过<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>多个<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">这个数字里内涵着本网所有工作人员在高度风险下的巨大付出。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">本报告之所以能够按时定期发布，并且信息越来越翔实，这也得到了大陆许多人权捍卫者的积极反馈和支持。本网对所有提供信息的朋友，在此一并予以感谢。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">九年多如一日，本网持续不断地对中国大陆政治犯、良心犯境况进行总结和报告，是为了抗议谴责中共当局以超期羁押、拖延审判、虐待折磨、殴打等各种方式对良心犯政治犯施加酷刑，而在中共狱中被酷刑虐待折磨是被关押者要经常面对的严酷现实。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">本网坚信，外界坚持不懈的关注，将会给狱中受难者以精神和实质的援助！本报告一直对中共当局使用各种酷刑手段迫害折磨政治犯、良心犯的行径予以的系统揭露，业已引起了海内外各个方面的强烈反响。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">本网一直在及时更新、统计最新讯息，每月末发布这月度报告，谨以此表达我们对所有失去自由的政治犯、良心犯的关注和牵挂。并以此，告诉全世界不要忘记这些为自由、民主、人权而承担苦难的人们。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">本网认为，本报告的定期更新和发布，可以直接反映出大陆当下的人权概况——因为一个国家的政治犯、良心犯的境况是这个国家最重要的人权指标之一。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">本网</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">以此</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">揭示中国大陆当下恶劣的人权概况与良心犯、政治犯的悲惨处境，力求唤起国际社会对中国在押政治犯、良心犯的记忆，并予以持续不断的关注和呼吁，直至他们获得自由。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">本网认为，定期将良心犯、政治犯的姓名和境况公诸于世，是我们能给予这些受难者以实际而有效支持的一种方式。我们深知，没有比被人们的遗忘更令这些良心犯、政治犯感到绝望和痛苦的事情。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">因此，我们必须肩负起这项工作，乃至是使命。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">九年多的风风雨雨已经过去，未来的道路上还会有千难万险，但是有你们的支持，我们仍将一如既往勇往直前！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">最后，本报告虽经本网信息中心认真核查，并得到中国大陆许多人权捍卫者协助，但仍因条件所限，无法做到适时、准确统计全部在押政治犯、良心犯信息，报告所反映的只是冰山之一角，仍然是一份不完全的报告，这需要我们的继续努力！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">如发现纰漏之处和补充信息，敬请指正，并尽可能知会本网。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">本网邮箱：</span></b></span></span><a href="mailto:wqw2011@gmail.com"><span style="mso-bookmark: class="MsoListParagraph" style="mso-list: l8 level1 lfo25; text-indent: -36.0pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">一、<span style="font: 7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span></b><!--[endif]--><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">本期报告概述：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告》月月更新，是一份关于中国在押政治犯、良心犯的动态报告。此为第<span lang="EN-US">113</span>期。至此，本报告月月发布历时已整整九年多。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">本期报告全文共计</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">五万五千字</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">。本期报告对上期报告的所有政治犯、良心犯名单进行了一次全面的逐一核查。获悉上期名单中</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">28</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">人已被</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">刑满释放或取保获释。并获悉有被羁押的<span lang="EN-US">1</span>人被判刑，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>人狱中有新动态；本期获悉有<span lang="EN-US">2</span>名良心犯狱中被迫害致死。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">同时，本期新增了我们又搜集的被刑事拘留<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人以及被判刑的<span lang="EN-US">47</span>人，合计<span lang="EN-US">49</span>人的名单及简介。目前，被本期报告录入姓名发布的在押良心犯、政治犯共</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">1700</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">人。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">为便于人们查询，《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯名单索引》为本报告名单的唯一索引。索引是以姓名拼音顺序排列（<span lang="EN-US">ABCDEFG....WXYZ</span>）。同时，本报告对所有良心犯、政治犯的刑期进行了统计，羁押未判的也全部列于最后。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><a _Hlk175727158;"></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk181147271;"></span><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">蔡伟华、蔡予华、陈治坤、董怡然、郭永凤、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">夏东梅、夏泽红、杨春林、杨兰英、臧中美、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span _Hlk162448506;"><a name="_Hlk167930243"></a><a name="_Hlk165272513"></a><a name="_Hlk167929814"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">1</span></b></span></span></a></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">、<a name="_Hlk191362820">蔡伟华</a>：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">女，哈尔滨市法轮功学员。大学本科毕业，从事财务统计工作多年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日过遭抓捕，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月初，蔡伟华被入黑龙江省女子监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">2</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">、蔡予华</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">：河南省三门峡市法轮功学员，女，二零二一年四月左右被判刑四年半，现已被劫持到河南省新乡女子监狱。蔡予华由于坚定修炼法轮功，在<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年前被中共劳教（具体时间不详）。蔡予华由于在<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月向最高法院和检察院邮寄控告迫害元凶江泽民的控告信，同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日晚上被抓捕、关押，家人被勒索财物，后又被判刑，在新乡女子监狱，受尽折磨，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年出狱。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，蔡予华向有关部门邮寄了申诉控告信，要求返还并按时发放她在判刑期间被剥夺的养老保险金。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月初，蔡予华被三门峡陕州区警察从家中抓捕，关押在三门峡市看守所，至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半，后被送往新乡女子监狱继续关押迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">3</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">、陈治坤：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">广东五华县法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1982</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月出生，重庆市铜梁区人，近年居住广东梅州市五华县。陈治坤于<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年读高一时开始修炼法轮功，大学毕业后曾经在梁平县中学任高中教师。<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，他被重庆市梁平县（现梁平区）警察抓捕，被劳教一年。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年，陈治坤在浙江省散发神韵光盘与《九评共产党》等真相资料被警察抓捕；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，他被浙江省台州市路桥法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，梅州市五华县公安局警察抓捕了陈治坤，称他散发法轮功资料，并对他抄家。次日，陈治坤被刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，他被五华县检察院批准逮捕，后被梅县区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金三万。陈治坤上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，梅州市中级法院驳回上诉，维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，郭永凤在贵阳市观山湖区给民众发放法轮功资料时遭人恶告，被警察抓捕。后郭永凤被关押在贵阳三江看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月获悉，郭永凤被中共法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，已被关押到贵州省第一女子监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被皇姑区黄河派出所、皇姑区国保警察抓捕构陷；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日在攀枝花市西区清香坪向世人发疫情刊物等法轮功资料时，被人诬告。<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日早上<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点左右，罗巧俐和罗巧萍同时在各自的居住处被抓捕。因为全家修炼法轮功，一直和父母住在一起的弟弟罗晓星及母亲也同时被抓捕。一直被关押在仁和区棉纱湾看守所。姐弟<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年并处罚金。罗巧萍刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: text1;">一名乡村医生，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生，行医<span lang="EN-US">4</span>。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年了，<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年开始修炼法轮大法，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日中共集团开始迫害法轮功以后，吕春钰因为坚持自己的信仰，告诉人们法轮功被迫害的真相，屡次被抓捕、骚扰迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，再次被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，吕春钰家属找律师去大连姚家看守所会见吕春钰，律师说：吕春钰已经被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，最近要送到监狱去，现在不让会见。现羁押在大连姚家看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; lang="EN-US">2022</span>年六十八岁。在中共对法轮功持续至今二十多年的迫害中，彭乐宽曾两次被判五年，遭<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年冤狱迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日（正月十五日）中午，在自己的家中被招远市泉山派出所的多个警察抓捕，后得知彭乐宽被栖霞法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">68</span>岁，原吉林省榆树市培英街道办事处司法助理员，后居住在长春市。因坚持修炼法轮功，在江泽民发动的对法轮功的迫害中，苏玉财曾九次被抓捕，四次被劳教。</span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span mso-themecolor: text1;"> </span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">2021</span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日早，苏玉财在送孙子上学，在学校门前被长春市长久派出所警察抓捕，后抄家。苏玉财在派出所，遭刑讯逼供，被强迫坐铁椅子。之后，苏玉财被送长春市苇子沟拘留所。因体检不合格，苏玉财被放回。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日晚，长久派出所再次抓捕了苏玉财。苏玉财被长春市朝阳区长久派出所关押三天，然后，被转入长春市第二看守所。此后，家人和朋友一直没有他的消息。直到<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年初，家人才得知，长春市朝阳区法院已于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月秘密对苏玉财判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<b text1;">14</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">、孙茜：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">加拿大华籍女富商。孙茜是北京利德曼生物化学公司的创始人，<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年获加拿大国籍，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年登上胡润中国富豪榜，身家<span lang="EN-US">35</span>亿。由于操劳过度，身体严重透支，孙茜患上多种疾病，多方医治无效。在<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年她学习炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，孙茜正在家中与表妹聊天，警方突然闯入抄家，搜出法轮功相关书籍后，将她抓捕。期间，孙茜多次遭受酷刑，被铐在铁椅子上，被辣椒水喷脸。全天被戴上镣铐，强制洗脑，强迫放弃她的信仰。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，孙茜一案在北京朝阳法院温榆河法庭开庭，孙茜获刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">15</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">黑龙江伊春市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年生，黑龙江省伊春市嘉荫县嘉荫农场退休职工，户籍所在地黑龙江省嘉荫县嘉荫农垦社区<span lang="EN-US">B</span>区<span lang="EN-US">9</span>委<span lang="EN-US">1</span>组<span lang="EN-US">246</span>号，现住址黑龙江省佳木斯市向阳区滨江小区<span lang="EN-US">2</span>期<span lang="EN-US">22</span>号楼<span lang="EN-US">3</span>单元<span lang="EN-US">402</span>室。王淑波女士于<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年开始修炼法轮功，王淑波于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日傍晚，在佳木斯市住处遭向阳公安分局松林派出所警察入室抓捕、关押构陷，两次庭审后，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，佳木斯市向阳区法院对其判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，其被关押在佳木斯市看守所。王淑波上诉到佳木斯市中级法院，中院维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月被关押至黑龙江女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b><span _Hlk167930243;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">女，云南</span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">昆明市法轮功学员<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月出生，云南省曲靖市马龙县人。她曾在昆明煤矿机械总厂马龙分厂经营一家理发店，后因修炼法轮功被非法劳教，理发店被迫关闭。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日在她家中被曲靖市马龙国保、昆明市盘龙国保抄家、抓捕，之后一直被关押在曲靖市麒麟区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，她遭麒麟区法院开庭并判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日送到云南省第二女子监狱继续遭受迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/28/444176.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span text1;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/28/444176.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">、臧中美：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1973</span>年生。吉林省白城法轮功学员。臧中美原是吉林省梨树农场一名小学女教师，<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年末因去北京上访被劳教一年半，释放回家后，丈夫和幼小的孩子因经受不住长期的警察上门骚扰被迫离婚。因她不放弃信仰，也被学校开除，流离失所到白城市打工。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，臧中美骑电瓶车宣讲法轮功被白城市洮北区国保大队抓捕，并在其住处抄走大法书籍、电脑、真相资料、现金等物品。后被批捕。曾正在看守所绝食反迫害。臧中美<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月份被秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，关押在长春女子监狱十三大队。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">67</span>岁，昆明市人，曾因修炼法轮功被判刑迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日下午，张晓华到官渡区子君路星云园小区朋友家串门，被警方抓捕，随后张晓华家被搜查。同时被抓捕的还有田云波、李萍等人。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日张晓华、李萍、田云波被五华区法院视频庭审，后被判刑：张晓华<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，李萍<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月，田云波<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被二道区荣光派出所四个人入室抓捕、抄家，随即遭刑事拘留，后遭批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月底获悉，她被长春朝阳法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>午，江北区寸滩派出所、江北区国保到渝北区天宫殿他的出租房，砸坏门锁，破门而入，抓捕了张礼江，并抄家。随即，张礼江被刑事拘留，关押在江北区复盛看守所，后被批捕、起诉，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">甘肃省庆阳市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年六十多岁，家住庆阳市西峰区董志镇。她因坚持真、善、忍信仰，经常遭中共官员及警察骚扰，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年她曾被判刑。曹稳梅女士<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月被警察抓捕后，。因当地看守以疫情为由拒收，曹稳梅当时得以回家。但正宁县公安局国保大队构陷当地检察院、法院，对曹稳梅进行司法迫害，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年初被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月获知，曹稳梅已被当地法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"></span><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">三、本期获悉狱中<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人的动态信息（附简历）<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><a name="_Hlk159665615"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">1</span></b></a></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">、危文元<span lang="EN-US">1</span>人被判刑：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></span></p><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"></span><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><a name="_Hlk170538828"></a><a name="_Hlk162565472"></a><a name="_Hlk189027184"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">4</span></b></span></span></a></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk189027184;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">年：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">危文元<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><a name="_Hlk191447282"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">危文元</span></b></a></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日出生，重庆市南岸区人，维权公民，公民记者。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，曾因所属房屋被政府强拆，一直未予公平公正的拆迁赔偿，遂被迫上访维权；期间，因多次投诉未果，且屡遭政府截访打压，随开始关注、投身于弱势群体的维权活动，同时认识到公民捍卫民主、自由、人权的重要性，故而成为重庆知名的公民记者，并积极帮助重庆访民进行维权报导和呼吁；曾因发布数百篇维权报导而遭遇当局的数十次威胁打压；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，曾因六四敏感时期而被警方关押<span lang="EN-US">5</span>天，并多处受伤；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，曾因与维权公民兼公民记者王晶、肖建芳等多人进京维权，并到世界互联网大会现场举牌呼吁“保障互联网自由，停止打压维权讯息传播”，而遭警方围堵截访，被遣返后又遭重庆警方非法施暴；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，曾因《重庆日报》报业集团涉嫌虚假报导，而与数十名维权公民和访民到该报社门前谴责抗议；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，曾因有访民电告在重庆报社有人跳楼，其前往围观，看见报社内外确有大量访民和警察存在，在调查暗访中，其被警方带走失联，后得知被重庆市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，又被重庆市渝中区警方以同罪名正式逮捕判刑；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，在被超期关押<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年半后，获释出狱此前被羁押于重庆市第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被抓捕，据称罪名是涉嫌寻衅滋事罪。危文元女士被捕前一直关注和支持黄琦母亲蒲文清女士，长期关注李怀庆案件，对包艳女士提供帮助和支持。两年多后，获悉其被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。目前在重庆女子监狱一监区服刑</span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span _Hlk170538828;"></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/02/4.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span
