text1;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/02/4.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">2</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">、</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">马彦、张盼成、张文鹏、谭兵林、丁中福、周松林、张春雷、徐秦等<span lang="EN-US">8</span>人狱中动态信息通报：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">1/</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">马彦：（</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，本网获悉遭羁押的银川市金凤区家庭教会传道人马彦的最新案情及简历，现在通报如下：</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;"> <span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">马彦：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">1992</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日出生，籍贯云南省昭通市镇雄县，宁夏回族自治区银川市西夏区居住公民，基督徒，银川市金凤区家庭教会传道人，中国在押良心犯。早年，曾在大学期间即接受了基督教信仰；毕业、工作后，因受感呼召就毅然到宁夏回族自治区银川市进行专职服事，在金凤区组建家庭教会做传道人；其因为人善良、满有爱心，遂在教会信众及经常被探访的基督徒家人眼里备受称许和信任；然而，因其所在教会未加入中共当局所属“三自”教会，故遭当局刻意冲击与打压；<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，当其与约<span lang="EN-US">10</span>名基督徒在银川市金凤区一间民宿中查经聚会时，突遭银川市金凤区警方和当地小区派出所警方等的连手冲击和抓捕，其中，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>名基督徒弟兄被以“以扰乱公共场所秩序”为由处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">7</span>天，而其及另一名弟兄被以同罪由处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天，并均被关押在银川市拘留所；<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，其家人虽收到金凤区警方对其的解除行政拘留通知书，但转而又被以涉嫌“组织非法聚集罪”刑事拘留，并直接送银川市看守所关押；三天之后，其家人发代祷信披露其等被拘留消息，并称“宪法规定了公民有宗教信仰自由，基督徒聚会不是非法聚集，更没有扰乱社会秩序”；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，其被银川市金凤区检察院以涉嫌“组织非法聚集罪”转正式批捕；后其案被起诉，并于<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被检察院移交至银川市金凤区法院；据悉，此期间，其尚有与此案相关的另一行政处罚案，银川铁路铁路运输法院和银川市中级法院一直拖延，既不立案也不回复，其委托律师称“这明显违反了《行政诉讼法》规定，也不符<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日最高人民法院发布的《关于在审判工作中促进提质增效推动实质性化解矛盾纠纷的指导意见》第三条，故向宁夏高级人民法院书面申请监督；<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，知其案在银川市金凤区法院开庭受理，但至今仍未宣判。目前被羁押于银川市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/02/blog-post_25.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/02/blog-post_25.html</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">2/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">张盼成：甘肃人权捍卫者<a name="_Hlk191394628">张盼成</a>狱中情况通报（<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日）<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，本网获悉：近日，有网友前去甘肃省合水县看守所试图给张盼成存钱和衣物，被看守所拒绝，说只有家属可以办理。此前张盼成父母和律师有亲自面签了委托协议，但当律尝试履行协议，又被看守所、警察和法院以张盼成父母不认可委托协议为由拒绝律师办案。目前律师没有会见到张盼成，也无法再联系上其父母。张盼成是于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被刑刑事拘留；此前曾两次因言获罪，被以寻衅滋事罪判刑，刑期共<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">张盼成简介：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">1995</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日出生，甘肃省庆阳市合水县人，网名为“子慕予兮”，中国西北农村长大的留守儿童，前北京大学保安，政治犯。早年出生于甘肃农村，是典型的留守儿童；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，曾以公民身份表达自己的意愿；在辞去北京大学保安工作之后，曾放胆自拍视频，发政治主张，称已为民主“做好了牺牲的准备”；被捕前，曾在视频中表示，不同意中国政府将<span lang="EN-US">600</span>亿美元未经法定程序送<span lang="EN-US">(</span>外国）人，要求言论自由，声援被失踪的董瑶琼、华涌、佳士工人和原北大学生岳昕等人，以及进学习班的百万新疆同胞；曾在视频中引用宋代名将文天祥的诗句“人生自古谁无死，留取丹心照汗青”，并说自己对国家有深沉的爱；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，被抓捕刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，被北京市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”正式逮捕；审讯中，拒绝写保证书，并拒绝给律师签委托书；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，其案在北京西城区法院开庭审理；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，被北京市西城区法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，刑满释放；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，因其在网上发布一段在甘肃山村老家里录制的视频，谴责中共暴行，表达心声称“凛凛寒冬终将过去，春天马上要来临”，遂被甘肃省合水县警方莫名刑拘，家遭查处，自此失联；后知又被当地合县检察院转正式批捕，被关押在甘肃省庆阳市合水县看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，知其已在两周前被甘肃省合水县法院一审秘判，但其家人未获判决书。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日获悉，其被以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。曾在甘肃省武都监狱服刑。张盼成于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日刑满释放，张盼成回到家中后，屡遭当地警方骚扰和监控，出行自由遭剥夺，甚至想强迫做精神病检查。张盼成迫于无奈，分别于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日和<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日就其状况发布了情况通报。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日的文中称，自己长期被跟踪，且身份证户口本均被没收，当地多次上门要将其认定为“精神病”，并表示如果自己再次被带走，将绝食抗议。后其遭强迫失踪，已失联多日，音信全无。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日获悉其被再次被刑事拘留。</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/02/2025225.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/02/2025225.html</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">3/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">张文鹏：海南三亚二看：禁止张文鹏阅卷、核对证据<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，本网获悉：近日，李国蓓律师前往三亚二看会见张文鹏并核对案件证据材料，三亚二看予以拒绝。张文鹏案已经移送检察机关，李国蓓律师业已阅卷；与当事人核对证据、让当事人查看案卷证据材料是法律规定的。然而三亚二看认为，案件重大敏感，看守所有规定不能过问案情，资料涉及证据内容，看守所不方便审查；况且也没有法律条款写明可以将阅卷资料交付给被告人，应当由办案单位审查并出具同意交付的书面证明。李国蓓律师对此提出书面控告。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">张文鹏简历：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">1993</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">31</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">23</span>岁大学毕业后，张文鹏就考取得律师资格证书，按照中国的法律规定，实习一年就能获得律师执业证书，但是他实习<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年了，一直无法获得执业证。原因是他一直在反对“官办律师协会”，上了司法部的黑名单，因此青岛市司法局一直刁难他，不给他执业证，一拖就是<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。张文鹏被律师界誉为著名实习律师的一条，他揭露律协的腐败，痛斥行贿律师，因此也得罪了一些既得利益者，以至于永久被禁止执业。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年张文鹏在网上发布了实名举报信，指控青岛司法局局长万振东行贿、挥霍公款、渎职等<span lang="EN-US">3</span>大罪责。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，在山东晓临律师事务所实习的张文鹏在微博发文称：<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，他在深圳被青岛市公安局市南分局跨省传唤，他被衣服扒光，内裤都不让穿，持续传唤八小时，理由是扰乱单位秩序。张文鹏到深圳本地派出所询问，了解到，跨省传唤的事由是“曾擅自闯入了青岛司法局”。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，张文鹏又因为代理海韵集团案件，帮助当事人喊冤，被三亚警方以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪予以刑事拘留。就在他被刑事拘留前，该案辩护人北大博士张庆方律师被通知将吊销律师执照。这显然就是三亚警方利用公权对海韵代理人予以打击报复。</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/02/blog-post_21.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/02/blog-post_21.html</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">4/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">谭兵林：获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月湖南人权捍卫者谭兵林已被转监至湖南省郴州监狱服刑<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，本网获悉：获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月湖南人权捍卫者谭兵林已被转监至湖南省郴州监狱服刑。谭兵林于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被以寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，后遭判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。谭兵林此前被羁押于祁东县看守所，现已被转监至湖南省郴州监狱服刑，电话<span lang="EN-US">0735-2193060</span>；<span lang="EN-US">0735-2193000</span>，邮编<span lang="EN-US">423000</span>。家属被告知需要所在镇政府领导帮助预约才能会见，目前家属还没有收到会见通知。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">谭兵林简介：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">湖南省衡阳市祁东县人，教育平权推动者，免费医疗、免费教育、免费养老（俗称“三免”）倡导者之一，维权公民，中国在押政治犯。近年来，曾因长期参与推动教育平权运动，倡导俗称“三免”的免费医疗、免费教育、免费养老的民生要求，以及以义工身份积极参与为良心犯送饭的公益活动等，而被社会正义人士和深受关怀帮助的弱势群体广为认可和赞许；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，曾因在老家湖南省祁东县步云桥镇几处重要地段（含市集中心地段、祁东县政府门口、县人大常委会门口等地）举牌要求民生“三免”，即免费医疗、免费教育、免费养老以及其它要求，遂被当地维稳办人员诱骗至镇政府扣押，后被祁东县警方带走调查；期间，尽管刚开始时被很快就被释放，但同天下午又被祁东县警方带走并恶意扣留<span lang="EN-US">4</span>天，要求其写保证书，保证以后不上街举牌，但被其拒绝；后祁东县教育局正副局长前来与其见面，就其举牌内容中提及的教育问题与其谈判；因其坚持向教育局长当面提出<span lang="EN-US">225 </span>个教育问题，终使对方被迫承诺回去后将就其中的<span lang="EN-US">16</span>个问题进行研讨更新，届时必向其作答；然而时至<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，其因一直未见教育局副局长所称的“不在学校吃饭的学生可以退伙食费”之公示，遂其前往步云桥<span lang="EN-US">3</span>所学校进行调查取证，结果不仅均未看到退款公示，反而遭到<span lang="EN-US">3</span>所校方人员的驱逐和拒绝；而与此同时，却有学生家长听闻其做实地调查，就向其反映说，学校里每天都卖垃圾食品，严重影响了孩子的身体健康，但校方却为自身利益而任由其发展；鉴此，其立即特发声明，呼吁和要求教育局务必让各学校在校门之外张贴退伙食费公示，否则其将于次日恢复上街举牌；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，因其获悉在押政治犯张展在狱中因绝食抗争而致生命垂危，故而毅然在步云桥镇街头再次勇敢举牌声援，以期能引起中共当局的重视，让病重中的张展获准保外就医；正是基于以上言行，其即引起湖南省衡阳市当局极度不满，并成为需要尽快维稳打压的对象；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，其因故前往海南省海口市，但在海口市火车站出站时却遭到防疫人员的拦截和要求强制做核酸检测；被其拒绝后，其身份证被扣，其本人被长时间限制在火车站不准出站；后经海南公民蓝采儿等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人到火车站为其声援，才终与海口火车站方达成协议，对方不再强制其做核酸检测，但必须被警方遣送回原籍；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，因其父母被强行接种新冠疫苗，其到村委会举牌抗议，遂立遭衡阳市祁东县警方抓捕，自此失联；同天其家被查抄，其个人手机和笔记本计算机等被一并抄走；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，其父获悉，其已于被抓当天被祁东县警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；后遭批捕，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日获悉其案件已经到了审判阶段。随后，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年年初已经开庭。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日获悉，谭兵林获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。此前被羁押于祁东县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月获悉，谭兵林已被转监至湖南省郴州监狱服刑。</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/02/46_20.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/02/46_20.html</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">5/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">丁中福：遭抓捕的安徽省合肥市基督教甘泉家庭教会长老丁中福的最新案情及简历</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，本网获悉遭抓捕的安徽省合肥市基督教甘泉家庭教会长老丁中福的案情及简历，现在通报如下：<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">丁中福：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">1960</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">年代出生，安徽省人，基督徒，安徽省合肥市甘泉家庭教会长老、教会财务管理负责人，家庭教育工作者，中国在押良心犯。因笃信耶稣基督，故自愿在教会里做服事工作，后被按立为长老并在安徽省合肥市甘泉教会作牧者同工<span lang="EN-US">; </span>因其正直良善、积极努力、追求公理正义的品性，并热心投身于家庭教育事业的心志，其在教会及周围小区受到许多人的好评，尤其是其在教会里通过言传身教说明了很多信徒建立和巩固良好的家庭关系<span lang="EN-US">; </span>然而，因其所在合肥甘泉教会虽历经<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多年的发展，已经扩充为已有四、五百信徒的当地知名度较高的家庭教会，故十年余来经常遭当地宗教局与警方的冲击与搅扰<span lang="EN-US">;2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其等<span lang="EN-US">16</span>名甘泉教会的牧者、同工突遭合肥市蜀山区警方统一上门传唤，所有人的家均被搜查，而后其与教会里的周松林牧师、茅骏马传道、裴德飞传道、管理同工杨佩云被以涉嫌“诈欺罪”刑事拘留<span lang="EN-US">;</span>同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，除<span lang="EN-US">3</span>位传道及同工被取保候审外，其和周松林牧师仍被续押，之后又被以同罪名转正式逮捕，指控其二人被抓捕与甘泉教会的两处房产和教会的资金流水有关，称其二人“以非法占有为目的，假借宗教名义，骗取他人钱财合计<span lang="EN-US">339</span>万余元，数额特别巨大”，故构成诈骗罪<span lang="EN-US">;2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其案被合肥市蜀山区警方移交到蜀山区法院要求起诉<span lang="EN-US">; </span>同年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月初，代理律师从蜀山区民警获悉，其案被通告：“<span lang="EN-US">1</span>、不会退侦了<span lang="EN-US">; 2</span>、延期半个月<span lang="EN-US">; 3</span>、不做认罪认罚了，因为两人都不认罪<span lang="EN-US">; 4</span>、不会超过<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日起诉到法院“<span lang="EN-US">; </span>此期间，其教会内部少数同工由于受到当局多方压力，而因其二人的妻子为他们聘请了不受当局欢迎的辩护律师，就产生了聘任分歧和分裂，导致部分信众表示要退出教会，对此，与其同案的周松林牧师于<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日从狱中称，其个人和丁中福长老此次遭受逼迫，“实属是一场政治逼迫”，不是他们“主动参与了政治，而是被迫卷入了政治”<span lang="EN-US">; </span>与此同时，两位被抓牧者的妻子亦发声明和呼吁称，自己的丈夫从“没有以欺骗手段非法占有他人财产，他们不是诈骗犯，他们是无辜的，请还给他们自由”<span lang="EN-US">; </span>另有多名教会信徒也在不同时间段为其二人被枉抓而向合肥市宗教局和刑侦队发出请愿书和写见证信，证明他们是冤枉的，不存在欺骗或诈骗，但官方均置之不理和不予相信<span lang="EN-US">;2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，其二人案在合肥市蜀山区人民法院召开庭前会议，因代理律师提出检察官没有履行应尽的职责，导致起诉书中存在诸多问题，故检察官当场被质疑得哑口无言，只得提前中止<span lang="EN-US">; </span>之后又于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日召开第二次庭前会议，但直至今日，其二人案仍然延审宣判<span lang="EN-US">;</span>据悉，其在看守所身体健康极度欠佳，除有老年人常见一些慢性病外，其血压最高时达到<span lang="EN-US">110-170</span>，加药也无法控制，常感胸闷、头晕和失眠，其妻子为夫呼吁“立即释放无罪之人”。目前被羁押于合肥看守所（安徽省合肥市长丰县双凤梅冲湖路监理支队合肥（男）看守所，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">230000</span>）。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/02/blog-post_11.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/02/blog-post_11.html</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">6/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">周松林：遭抓捕的安徽省合肥市甘泉家庭教会创办人周松林牧师的最新案情及简历</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，本网获悉遭抓捕的安徽省合肥市甘泉家庭教会创办人周松林牧师的最新案情及简历，现在通报如下：<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">周松林：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">1960</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">年代出生，安徽省人，基督徒，原为三自教会传道人，安徽省合肥市甘泉家庭教会创办人、牧师，中国在押良心犯。早于<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多年前，其曾在中国一神学院（政府认可）毕业后被分配到三自教会管辖下的一家教堂担任传道，但婚后因其与妻子倍感呼召，遂毅然离开三自教会（属体制内的“铁饭碗”），到安徽省合肥市创办了甘泉家庭教会，自此经其等全职侍奉、努力传讲福音，截至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年，甘泉教会已达四、五百名基督信徒；但因近<span lang="EN-US">10</span>余年来中共当局对家庭教会不断逼迫，各地家庭教会纷纷遭打压、被解散，其所在教会亦多次被迫搬迁，故为了敬拜活动免受冲击和搅扰，经教会同工大会决议，使用多年积累下来的信众奉献款购得两处教会房产，以作敬拜聚会活动使用；同时，为避免家庭教会房产不被中共当局承认，遂集体推举出几位同工共同持有（即将此两处房产写在该教会丁中福长老及另两名教会成员名下），且通过法律程序，视频公证存档，以证该房产属于教会财产，财产状况清晰；然而，此举却成为日后教会牧者、同工被当局派人抓捕、起诉的理由和罪证；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其等<span lang="EN-US">16</span>名甘泉教会的牧者、同工突遭合肥市蜀山区警方统一上门传唤，家均被搜查，而后其与丁中福长老、茅骏马传道、裴德飞传道、管理同工杨佩云被以涉嫌“诈骗罪”刑事拘留；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，除<span lang="EN-US">3</span>位传道和同工被取保候审外，其和丁中福长老仍被续押，而后又被转正式逮捕，指控其二人被抓捕与甘泉教会的两处房产和教会的资金流水有关；<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月初，其代理律师到合肥市蜀山区检察院获悉，其案当时情况：“<span lang="EN-US">1</span>、不会退侦了；<span lang="EN-US">2</span>、延期半个月；<span lang="EN-US">3</span>、不做认罪认罚了，因为二人都不认罪；<span lang="EN-US">4</span>、不会超过<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日起诉到法院”；此期间，其教会内部部分同工（或自称同工）由于受到当局多方压力，而因其二人之妻为他们聘请了当局不欢迎的辩护律师，就产生了聘任分歧和分裂，导致部分信众表示要退出教会，对此，其于<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日从狱中回应称，其个人和丁中福长老此次遭受逼迫，实属是一场政治逼迫，“不是他们主动参与了政治，而是被迫卷入了政治”；其妻子亦发声明，称其丈夫“是一名正直、敬虔的基督徒，全职服侍教会已有<span lang="EN-US">32</span>年之久，侍奉宗旨是：忠于上帝，本于圣经，高举基督，爱神爱人”，并且“为避免试探，他坚持自己在侍奉中不碰教会的钱财”，“没有一分钱落入自己的腰包”；同时呼吁，其牧师丈夫和丁中福长老“没有以欺骗手段非法占有他人财产，他们不是诈骗犯，他们是无辜的，请还给他们自由”；另有两名教会信徒也在不同时间段为其二人被枉抓而向合肥市宗教局和刑侦队发出请愿书和写见证材料，但官方置之不理和不予采信；<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，其被控诈骗罪案在合肥市蜀山区人民法院召开庭前会议，因代理律师提出检察官没有履行应尽的职责，导致起诉书存在诸多问题，故检察官当场被质问得哑口无言，只得提前中止会议；后又于同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日召开第二次庭前会议，但直至今日，其案仍无庭审结果；据悉，其在看守所虽身体健康欠佳，但学会了用三种心态生活，即殉道的心态、修道的心态、宣道的心态，并传话鼓励教会信众要“立定心志，为福音而活”。目前被羁押于合肥看守所（合肥市长丰县双凤梅冲湖路监管支队合肥（男）看守所，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">230000</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/02/blog-post_54.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/02/blog-post_54.html</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">7/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">张春雷：获刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年的贵阳仁爱归正教会张春雷长老去年底已被转监至贵州省王武监狱<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，本网获悉：获刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年的贵阳仁爱归正教会张春雷长老去年底已被转监至贵州省王武监狱，王武监狱是贵州省重刑犯监狱，通信地址：贵州省贵阳市经济技术开发区松花江路<span lang="EN-US">37</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">550009</span>。贵阳仁爱归正教会张春雷长老被控“煽动颠覆国家政权罪、诈骗罪”一案于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日在贵州省贵阳市中级人民法院进行宣判，张春雷长老被判处煽动颠覆国家政权罪三年六个月，诈骗罪两年，合并执行五年有期徒刑，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日止。张春雷长老不服一审判决，依法上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日贵州省高院维持了贵阳市中院以煽颠罪和诈骗罪名义对张春雷长老五年有期徒刑的判决。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">张春雷简历：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">1964</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月出生<span lang="EN-US">, </span>贵州省人，基督徒，贵阳市仁爱归正家庭教会主要组建人，教会带领人、长老，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年《牧者联署：为基督信仰的声明》首批签名人之一，中国在押良心犯。早年，曾因笃信耶稣基督，为广传基督教福音而与人共同组建了不从中共“三自教会”的“仁爱归正教会”；起初，该教会仅有几十会众，但在其不懈努力和事工（即神职人员在教会里所做的服务）带领下，因能热情广泛接待南来北往的信徒，故而在后来的国度事工中起到和发挥了重要的作用；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，曾因积极参与由四川成都王怡牧师发起的《牧者联署：为基督信仰的声明》的首批联署签名，随遭贵阳当局的严管监控；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其教会被贵阳市南明区民族宗教事务局突然取缔，并被指称，因其等一行人“未经批准，擅自以‘仁爱归正教会’名义在南明区中天商务港设立宗教场所，组织、举行宗教活动，接受宗教性捐献，违反《宗教事务条例》相关规定，责令停止宗教活动，拆除相关设施和标识”，最终致使其及教会信徒在失去会堂后只能在餐厅、酒店进行主日敬拜；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，曾因在当地某酒店举行主日聚会，而被数十名宗教局人员及警方先后<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次连手冲击，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次被封门，敬拜所用的十字架被强摘，其计算机等用品被查收；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，曾因其教会新租房屋的房东再次被当局威胁，故而其被逼无奈只得再次从新租的房屋搬走；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，因其教会有十数名信众在参加小组学习时被突然闯入的贵阳市南明区民宗局人员和警方带走，遂其赶到派出所与警方交涉要人，不料竟遭粗暴野蛮对待，并被以“非法经营社团”为由处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">11</span>天；拘留期满时，又被贵阳市云岩区警方以涉嫌“诈骗罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被贵阳市云岩区检察院以同罪名正式批捕；据悉，其妻子、儿子受牵连曾遭警方长时讯问且其妻遭虐待，教会多位同工成员亦遭抄家；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，其代理律师数次要求会见均受阻，被告知其“因涉嫌危害国家安全，在侦查期间未得到办案单位允许的情况下，禁止律师会见”。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年初遭起诉。于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日开庭，未宣判张春雷长老被控“煽动颠覆国家政权罪、诈骗罪”一案于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">10:00</span>在贵州省贵阳市中级人民法院进行宣判，张春雷长被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。此前张春雷长老被羁押于贵阳市第二看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年底转监至贵州省王武监狱服刑</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/02/5.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/02/5.html</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">8/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">徐秦：获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年的江苏人权捍卫者徐秦女士狱中情况通报——每天被要求学习习近平的治国理政方针和党史<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，本网获悉刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年的江苏人权捍卫者徐秦女士狱中情况，现在通报如下：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，徐秦家属在当地信访办、村支书、派出所多个人员“陪同”下去监狱探视了徐秦，徐秦说她每天被要求学习习近平的治国理政方针和党史，身体方面有比较明显的气喘症状，徐秦将于今年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日刑满。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">徐秦简历：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">女，民间维权组织“中国人权观察”前秘书长，“玫瑰团队”成员，人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。长期以来，一直关注中国人权状况，并与著名人权活动家、民主异议人士秦永敏一道筹建中国人权观察；自秦永敏被捕、秦之妻子赵素利“被失踪”后，她曾多次上街声援，跟进案件；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，被警方突然限制自由，之后一直遭跟踪与监控；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其在从扬州高邮到昆山的途中被警方带走，后得知其被扬州市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其家属委托的代理律师要求会见，遭到警方拒绝，但被告知其已于<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日由刑拘转为“指定居所监视居住”；<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，又被追加罪名，以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”继续扣留，且不准律师会见；据悉，此次被捕，皆与其近年来坚持关注人权问题，后又积极组织联署声援维权律师余文生，以及为维权公民徐琳筹款等活动有关；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日获悉，其已获取保释放；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，徐秦突然又被警方从家中带走；据悉，之前其案件一直处于延审中；此次被捕前，徐秦刚做完心脏搭桥手术，且患有脑梗、心梗、高血压等多种疾病。狱中身体状况急剧恶化，甚至瘫痪无法站立。后在律师的抗争和各界关注下，徐秦身体比以前好了一些，在别人的搀扶下可以走一小会。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月份看守所安排她到东方医院做了检查，开了一些药。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日徐秦案已经在扬州市看守所法庭召开庭前会议，但长时间仍不开庭审理。徐秦案被延期审理竟然达到十二次，中共政权玩弄法律的肆无忌惮，令世人叹为观止。徐秦案终于在<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日上午于扬州市中级人民法院开庭宣判，法庭判决徐秦犯煽动颠覆国家政权罪，处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。目前徐秦被羁押于江苏省扬州市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日进京维权，于<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日遭北京市公安局西城分局刑事拘留。先拘押在北京西城区看守所，后转交陕西渭南警方，目前羁押在陕西渭南市临渭区看守所。去年，吴永强实名举报陕西纪委书记王兴宁，充当黑恶势力保护伞等问题。此前，吴永强因反腐遭陕西当局强权打击报复。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被宣布给予开除党籍、撤职处分后，他向公安厅党委、陕西省委组织部申请申诉。期间，被公安厅人事处多次要求强行谈话，遭吴永强拒绝。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">尹登珍原是湖北省十堰市堰中蔬菜批发市场的个体工商户，由政府充当保护伞的恶霸看到其生意红火兴旺，强行断其财路，造成巨额损失而上访维权。因为上访，尹登珍在<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年被当局以“敲诈勒索政府”为名判刑三年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">尹登珍在<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年春节前遭十堰市郧阳区警察暴力绑架回地方后，已被郧阳区公安局以“扰乱单位秩序”罪名刑事拘留，并很快被郧阳区检察院批准逮捕。此前，尹登珍已因该罪名被北京市朝阳区小红门派出所行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，这次郧阳区警方又以同一件事同一罪名再次处罚，属于“一事两罚”。并且郧阳区警方是在没有任何合法手续的情况下把尹登珍从北京绑架回地方。从尹登珍的遭遇可以看出，地方警察已经黑帮化，为维稳不择手段。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: lang="EN-US">2</span>个月：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">杨将威、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">1/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">吕桂玲：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">山东威海市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年已经<span lang="EN-US">64</span>岁。山东威海市温泉镇江家寨人。她于一九九六年八月开始修炼法轮功。中共在全中国残酷迫害法轮功后，全国民众被中共谎言宣传洗脑和强制参与诬陷法轮功，为了还百姓的知情权，当时<span lang="EN-US">42</span>岁的威海市法轮功学员吕桂玲，配合其他三位法轮功学员黄敏、张乐金和姜鲁广，于<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年，在威海荣成、乳山、文登等地电视网络成功插播法轮功电视片。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月份，吕桂玲在外地被抓捕，后被关押在威海市看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，并被威海环翠区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">19</span>年。因其身体状况太差，曾被保外就医一段时间，后又遭收监。自<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月之后，家人就没有吕桂玲的音讯，山东省女子监狱不允许吕桂玲给家人打电话，也不允许家人探视。据悉，吕桂玲早已被迫害得满头白发，牙齿全都脱落，心脏肺部等器官出现危险。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年，吕桂腿疼得不能走路，一个多月后才好转。即使按照中共的判决，吕桂玲的刑期应该在<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月结束，因为按照现行法律，保外就医期间算刑期。可是至今，吕桂玲仍被关押着，预计她刑期大约至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/02/19.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/02/19.html</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><a name="_Hlk191445832"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">2/</span></b></a></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk191445832;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">唐高峰</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">1955</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日出生，化名「唐民富」、「唐富民」<span lang="EN-US">,</span>四川省南充市人，四川省德阳市旌阳区文庙街<span lang="EN-US">51</span>号居住公民，原德阳鑫科木业公司退休职工，民主宪政追求者，中国民主胜利党（属秘密组党）创建人，「泸州<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>大抓捕案」受害者，中国在押政治犯。早年即心生对中国民主自由理念的追求；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年，其曾有幸出国工作生活，并在此阶段接触和深入了解到西方民主国家在政治制度上的优越性，自此产生了在中国境内也应努力尝试产生新型民主党派，以促进祖国走向真正的民主宪政之路的构想，并为此自我率先设定了新型党派的名称「中国民主胜利党」（下称「民胜党」）以及党纲、党章与党徽；后于<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年起，其开始在网络上广交朋友，并与理念相合、热忱积极且有较强行动力的志同道合者王一飞、王威、刘振刚、周丹、代露等数人共同筹建「民胜党」；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年，因其提供资金让王威等人在国内寻找一处首届中央委员会召开地点，故至<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月初，其及王一飞、王威等多个核心人物在四川省成都市成华区一出租房内召开了该党派第一届中央委员会，会议由其主持，表决通过了「民胜党」旨在推翻中国共产党领导，改变社会主义制度等纲领性文件，确立了组织管理架构，由其任主席，王威任副主席，其他人等分别担任组织部长、军事部长、农民部长等职务；会后，其等所有该党成员开始依照组织纲领及其指使，赴境外寻求注册、发展组织成员、宣传反独裁体制思想；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年期间，由其出资<span lang="EN-US">40</span>余万元，其及核心成员（如王一飞、王威、刘振刚、周丹、代露等）为使组织发展卓有成效，并努力在脸书（<span lang="EN-US">Facebook</span>）、推特（<span lang="EN-US">Twitter</span>）等国际网络交流平台及境外媒体网站（如博讯网等）宣传「民胜党」成立的讯息、政治纲领和宗旨，并不断发展组织成员，直至<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年初，其因国内政治形势变得愈发恶劣而被迫停止资助，但各人仍不予余力利用不同管道宣传和发展「民胜党」的成果；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年，其等行为被中共当局暗查知晓，因之前该组织在四川泸州召开过第一届中央委员会，遂立即组成全国重大项目小组，由四川泸州警方统一实施抓捕行动，其等十数人纷纷被抓，而其作首要分子于<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日亦被泸州市警方以非法组建和发展「中国民主胜利党」为由拘捕，后被指定居所监视居住；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，被以涉嫌「颠覆国家政权罪」转为刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，又被泸州市检察院予以正式批捕，指控其因自身曲折经历而「对社会主义制度和国家体制心生不满」，与多人秘密组建反对政党，且其是发起人，组织和策划了“民胜党”的成立和第一次中央委员会的召开，提供资金，故已构成颠覆国家政权罪；<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日获悉，其等<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人涉嫌颠覆案被四川省泸州市中级法院一审分别宣判，其被以「颠覆国家政权罪」重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，没收个人财产<span lang="EN-US">50</span>万元；另有其他<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人，亦被以同罪名重判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年不等刑期；其等不服，均提起上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，经四川省高等法院二审裁决，其等均被驳回上诉，维持原判，其个人刑期预至<span lang="EN-US">2035</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月。值得一提的是，因其等<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人自抓捕后均被迫失联<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，几乎所有家属都没收到任何法律文书或通知，且不被允许见当事人及申请代理律师，只有恐吓及威胁，故一直对外鲜为人知。目前被羁押于四川泸州市看守所。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/02/12.html"><span _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><a name="_Hlk191434757"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: text1;">尹福英</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">吉林市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年已<span lang="EN-US">70</span>岁，原吉林市毛纺厂职工。在中共疯狂法轮功的二十多年中，她遭到吉林市“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”、丰满公安局、江南派出所、江南街道办、江南长城社区及吉林市毛纺厂等机构、单位的各种迫害，她曾被拘留三次，劳教两次，并被吉林市毛纺厂开除公职。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，吉林市“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”和吉林市国保大队及吉林市各区派出所警察、社区不法人员，有预谋，有计划地跨区按名单绑架了<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多位法轮功学员。法轮功学员尹福英女士也于当天被抓捕、抄家，后被关押在吉林市看守所。后获悉其被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2032</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/02/9.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family:
